93→\n    94→// Run ServiceImpl.\n    95→func (s *ServiceImpl) Run(ctx context.Context) error {\n    96→\t<-ctx.Done()\n    97→\treturn ctx.Err()\n    98→}\n    99→\n   100→// QueryData processes queries and returns query responses. It handles queries to single or mixed datasources, as well as expressions.\n   101→func (s *ServiceImpl) queryData(ctx context.Context, user identity.Requester, skipDSCache bool, reqDTO dtos.MetricRequest, supportLocaltimeRange bool) (*backend.QueryDataResponse, error) {\n   102→\tfromAlert := false\n   103→\tfor header, val := range s.headers {\n   104→\t\tif header == models.FromAlertHeaderName && val == \"true\" {\n   105→\t\t\tfromAlert = true\n   106→\t\t}\n   107→\t}\n   108→\t// Parse the request into parsed queries grouped by datasource uid\n   109→\tparsedReq, err := s.parseMetricRequest(ctx, user, skipDSCache, reqDTO, supportLocaltimeRange)\n   110→\tif err != nil {\n   111→\t\treturn nil, err\n   112→\t}\n   113→\n   114→\t// If there are expressions, handle them and return\n   115→\tif parsedReq.hasExpression || fromAlert {\n   116→\t\treturn s.handleExpressions(ctx, user, parsedReq)\n   117→\t}\n   118→\t// If there is only one datasource, query it and return\n   119→\tif len(parsedReq.parsedQueries) == 1 {\n   120→\t\treturn s.handleQuerySingleDatasource(ctx, user, parsedReq)\n   121→\t}\n   122→\t// If there are multiple datasources, handle their queries concurrently and return the aggregate result\n   123→\treturn s.executeConcurrentQueries(ctx, user, skipDSCache, reqDTO, parsedReq.parsedQueries)\n   124→}\n   125→\n   126→func (s *ServiceImpl) QueryData(ctx context.Context, user identity.Requester, skipDSCache bool, reqDTO dtos.MetricRequest) (*backend.QueryDataResponse, error) {\n   127→\treturn s.queryData(ctx, user, skipDSCache, reqDTO, false)\n   128→}\n   129→\n   130→func (s *ServiceImpl) QueryDataNew(ctx context.Context, user identity.Requester, skipDSCache bool, reqDTO dtos.MetricRequest) (*backend.QueryDataResponse, error) {\n   131→\treturn s.queryData(ctx, user, skipDSCache, reqDTO, true)\n   132→}\n   133→\n   134→// splitResponse contains the results of a concurrent data source query - the response and any headers\n   135→type splitResponse struct {\n   136→\tresponses backend.Responses\n   137→\theader    http.Header\n   138→}\n   139→\n   140→// executeConcurrentQueries executes queries to multiple datasources concurrently and returns the aggregate result.\n   141→func (s *ServiceImpl) executeConcurrentQueries(ctx context.Context, user identity.Requester, skipDSCache bool, reqDTO dtos.MetricRequest, queriesbyDs map[string][]parsedQuery) (*backend.QueryDataResponse, error) {\n   142→\tg, ctx := errgroup.WithContext(ctx)\n   143→\tg.SetLimit(s.concurrentQueryLimit) // prevent too many concurrent requests\n   144→\trchan := make(chan splitResponse, len(queriesbyDs))\n   145→\n   146→\t// Create panic recovery function for loop below\n   147→\trecoveryFn := func(queries []*simplejson.Json) {\n   148→\t\tif r := recover(); r != nil {\n   149→\t\t\tvar err error\n   150→\t\t\ts.log.Error(\"query datasource panic\", \"error\", r, \"stack\", log.Stack(1))\n   151→\t\t\tif theErr, ok := r.(error); ok {\n   152→\t\t\t\terr = theErr\n   153→\t\t\t} else if theErrString, ok := r.(string); ok {\n   154→\t\t\t\terr = errors.New(theErrString)\n   155→\t\t\t} else {\n   156→\t\t\t\terr = fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected error - %s\", s.cfg.UserFacingDefaultError)\n   157→\t\t\t}\n   158→\t\t\t// Due to the panic, there is no valid response for any query for this datasource. Append an error for each one.\n   159→\t\t\trchan <- buildErrorResponses(err, queries)\n   160→\t\t}\n   161→\t}\n   162→\n   163→\t// Query each datasource concurrently\n   164→\tfor _, queries := range queriesbyDs {\n   165→\t\trawQueries := make([]*simplejson.Json, len(queries))\n   166→\t\tfor i := 0; i < len(queries); i++ {\n   167→\t\t\trawQueries[i] = queries[i].rawQuery\n   168→\t\t}\n   169→\t\tg.Go(func() error {\n   170→\t\t\tsubDTO := reqDTO.CloneWithQueries(rawQueries)\n   171→\t\t\t// Handle panics in the datasource qery\n   172→\t\t\tdefer recoveryFn(subDTO.Queries)\n   173→\n   174→\t\t\tctxCopy := contexthandler.CopyWithReqContext(ctx)\n   175→\t\t\tsubResp, err := s.QueryData(ctxCopy, user, skipDSCache, subDTO)\n   176→\t\t\tif err == nil {\n   177→\t\t\t\treqCtx, header := contexthandler.FromContext(ctxCopy), http.Header{}\n   178→\t\t\t\tif reqCtx != nil {\n   179→\t\t\t\t\theader = reqCtx.Resp.Header()\n   180→\t\t\t\t}\n   181→\t\t\t\trchan <- splitResponse{subResp.Responses, header}\n   182→\t\t\t} else {\n   183→\t\t\t\t// If there was an error, return an error response for each query for this datasource\n   184→\t\t\t\trchan <- buildErrorResponses(err, subDTO.Queries)\n   185→\t\t\t}\n   186→\t\t\treturn nil\n   187→\t\t})\n   188→\t}\n   189→\n   190→\tif err := g.Wait(); err != nil {\n   191→\t\treturn nil, err\n   192→\t}\n   193→\tclose(rchan)\n   194→\tresp := backend.NewQueryDataResponse()\n   195→\treqCtx := contexthandler.FromContext(ctx)\n   196→\tfor result := range rchan {\n   197→\t\tfor refId, dataResponse := range result.responses {\n   198→\t\t\tresp.Responses[refId] = dataResponse\n   199→\t\t}\n   200→\t\tif reqCtx != nil {\n   201→\t\t\tfor k, v := range result.header {\n   202→\t\t\t\tfor _, val := range v {\n   203→\t\t\t\t\tif !slices.Contains(reqCtx.Resp.Header().Values(k), val) {\n   204→\t\t\t\t\t\treqCtx.Resp.Header().Add(k, val)\n   205→\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n   206→\t\t\t\t\t\ts.log.Warn(\"skipped duplicate response header\", \"header\", k, \"value\", val)\n   207→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   208→\t\t\t\t}\n   209→\t\t\t}\n   210→\t\t}\n   211→\t}\n   212→\n   213→\treturn resp, nil\n   214→}\n   215→\n   216→// buildErrorResponses applies the provided error to each query response in the list. These queries should all belong to the same datasource.\n   217→func buildErrorResponses(err error, queries []*simplejson.Json) splitResponse {\n   218→\ter := backend.Responses{}\n   219→\tfor _, query := range queries {\n   220→\t\ter[query.Get(\"refId\").MustString(\"A\")] = backend.DataResponse{\n   221→\t\t\tError: err,\n   222→\t\t}\n   223→\t}\n   224→\treturn splitResponse{er, http.Header{}}\n   225→}\n   226→\n   227→func QueryData(ctx context.Context, log log.Logger, dscache datasources.CacheService, exprService *expr.Service, reqDTO dtos.MetricRequest,   245→\n   246→// handleExpressions handles queries when there is an expression.\n   247→func (s *ServiceImpl) handleExpressions(ctx context.Context, user identity.Requester, parsedReq *parsedRequest) 282→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"expression request error: %w\", err)\n   283→\t}\n   284→\treturn qdr, nil\n   285→}\n   286→\n   287→// handleQuerySingleDatasource handles one or more queries to a single datasource\n   288→func (s *ServiceImpl) handleQuerySingleDatasource(ctx context.Context, user identity.Requester, parsedReq *parsedRequest) (*backend.QueryDataResponse, error) {\n   289→\tqueries := parsedReq.getFlattenedQueries()\n   290→\tds := queries[0].datasource\n   291→\tif err := s.dataSourceRequestValidator.Validate(ds, nil); err != nil {\n   292→\t\treturn nil, This function binds the incoming `dtos.MetricRequest` and can route requests to either the legacy query handler or the new query service based on feature flags.\\n\\n## Query Service (Core Logic)\\nThe `pkg/services/query/query.go` file implements the main `ServiceImpl` service. Key methods include:\\n- `queryData()`: Main query processing logic that parses requests, handles expressions, and dispatches to datasources\\n- `parseMetricRequest()`: Parses incoming queries and groups them by datasource UID\\n- `handleQuerySingleDatasource()`: Handles queries to a single datasource by building a `backend.QueryDataRequest` and calling the plugin client\\n- `handleExpressions()`: Processes expression queries through the expression service\\n- `executeConcurrentQueries()`: Handles concurrent queries across multiple datasources\\n\\n## Plugin Backend Query Dispatch\\nThe plugin client hierarchy for dispatching queries to backend plugins:\\n1. `pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go` implements the `plugins.Client` interface with `QueryData()` method that gets a plugin from the registry and calls its QueryData method\\n2. `pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client_v2.go` contains `ClientV2` which implements the actual gRPC communication. The `QueryData()` method converts backend requests to proto format using `backend.ToProto().QueryDataRequest()`, sends them via gRPC to the plugin, and converts responses back using `backend.FromProto().QueryDataResponse()`\\n3. `pkg/registry/apis/query/client/plugin.go` contains `pluginClient` which implements the query data client for the query service flow. It converts `data.QueryDataRequest` to `backend.QueryDataRequest`, gets plugin context via the provider, and calls the plugin client\\n\\n## Query Response Transformation\\nQuery responses are transformed through multiple layers:\\n1. `pkg/expr/query_convert.go` provides `ConvertBackendRequestToDataRequest()` to convert backend query requests to k8s API format for multi-tenant query service flows\\n2. `pkg/expr/transform.go` implements expression transformation via `TransformData()`, which builds and executes an expression pipeline\\n3. `pkg/expr/service.go` contains the `Service` struct that orchestrates expression evaluation\\n\\n## K8s API Registry Handler\\nThe query service is also exposed as a K8s API:\\n1. `pkg/registry/apis/query/query.go` implements `queryREST` which handles query requests through the k8s REST API\\n2. The `Connect()` method returns an HTTP handler that binds query requests and calls `handleQuery()`\\n3. `handleQuery()` converts k8s query requests to the internal `dtos.MetricRequest` format and calls `service.QueryData()`\\n4. `pkg/registry/apis/query/register.go` contains `QueryAPIBuilder` which registers the query service in the k8s API server\\n\\n## Plugin Context Provider\\n`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/plugincontext/plugincontext.go` provides the `Provider` service which supplies plugin context information including plugin metadata and datasource instance settings via methods like `GetWithDataSource()`.\\n\\n## Query Models and Configuration\\n`pkg/services/query/models.go` defines key data structures:\\n- `parsedQuery`: Represents a parsed query with datasource and backend query information\\n- `parsedRequest`: Groups parsed queries by datasource UID\\n\\nThe complete query path flows from HTTP request -> QueryMetricsV2 -> queryData -> parseMetricRequest -> handleQuerySingleDatasource -> pluginClient.QueryData -> gRPC dispatch to plugin -> response transformation and return.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
